1307         tmp2 = ptr->\hyperlink{structpermonst_a8a558cbb5f8985df95bffa4439856374}{mattk}[i].\hyperlink{structattack_a0836728d155c969f6b43814c6a200ccd}{aatyp};
1308         n += (tmp2 > 0);
1309         n += (tmp2 == \hyperlink{monattk_8h_aae08f3175f1d778d2656ec379266fc49}{AT\_MAGC});
1310         n += (tmp2 == \hyperlink{monattk_8h_a6db6784344c2424d385f6b460f0c029f}{AT\_WEAP} && (ptr->\hyperlink{structpermonst_ad620729c9694b29047996af4e5380030}{mflags2} & \hyperlink{monflag_8h_a4a0727d8dcbbc504a7f3acaf0051350a}{M2\_STRONG}));
1311     \}
1312 
1313 \textcolor{comment}{/*  For each "special" damage type */}
1314     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(i = 0; i < \hyperlink{permonst_8h_af9119a416b08e0f343f33a0a7a945e93}{NATTK}; i++) \{
1315 
1316         tmp2 = ptr->\hyperlink{structpermonst_a8a558cbb5f8985df95bffa4439856374}{mattk}[i].\hyperlink{structattack_a14286742d9dc1310f5c4852432264080}{adtyp};
1317         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((tmp2 == \hyperlink{monattk_8h_a4c57ec4f6d96ffb69d5dd9ec95a2197b}{AD\_DRLI}) || (tmp2 == \hyperlink{monattk_8h_acd88c8b5dc08b255aa9a34768f7efb7c}{AD\_STON}) || (tmp2 == 
      \hyperlink{monattk_8h_a0ad77a3f1ad018dfbe3cb1fdad8558a7}{AD\_DRST})
1318         || (tmp2 == \hyperlink{monattk_8h_a3151d76132b61d1753b0dfdef9b2a8f4}{AD\_DRDX}) || (tmp2 == \hyperlink{monattk_8h_abe7238949c34d3575389cb995e764cc3}{AD\_DRCO}) || (tmp2 == 
      \hyperlink{monattk_8h_a74a7c164c0252682b319ae986e88b48a}{AD\_WERE}))
1319             n += 2;
1320         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (strcmp(ptr->\hyperlink{structpermonst_ae92da7d141243d7e37d4a12340bb248f}{mname}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"grid bug"})) n += (tmp2 != \hyperlink{monattk_8h_a9191d6bf636e5ada34fa9169ecaa4d9a}{AD\_PHYS});
1321         n += ((int) (ptr->\hyperlink{structpermonst_a8a558cbb5f8985df95bffa4439856374}{mattk}[i].\hyperlink{structattack_ac2b210543d1c0d0db89106b7d5f9ee00}{damd} * ptr->\hyperlink{structpermonst_a8a558cbb5f8985df95bffa4439856374}{mattk}[i].\hyperlink{structattack_abf8c529d3dc814dcbe98780aaa9a9194}{damn}) > 23);
1322     \}
1323 
1324 \textcolor{comment}{/*  Leprechauns are special cases.  They have many hit dice so they}
1325 \textcolor{comment}{    can hit and are hard to kill, but they don't really do much damage. */}
1326     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!strcmp(ptr->\hyperlink{structpermonst_ae92da7d141243d7e37d4a12340bb248f}{mname}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"leprechaun"})) n -= 2;
1327 
1328 \textcolor{comment}{/*  Finally, adjust the monster level  0 <= n <= 24 (approx.) */}
1329     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(n == 0) tmp--;
1330     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(n >= 6) tmp += ( n / 2 );
1331     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} tmp += ( n / 3 + 1);
1332 
1333     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}((tmp >= 0) ? tmp : 0);
1334 \}
\end{DoxyCode}
